663/* Relocate STACK from its old location to the new one. The
664 local variables YYSIZE and YYSTACKSIZE give the old and new number of
665 elements in the stack, and YYPTR gives the new location of the
666 stack. Advance YYPTR to a properly aligned location for the next
667 stack. */
668# define YYSTACK_RELOCATE(Stack_alloc, Stack) \
669 do \
670 { \
671 YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int yynewbytes; \
672 YYCOPY (&yyptr->Stack_alloc, Stack, yysize)__builtin_memcpy (&yyptr->Stack_alloc, Stack, (yysize)
* sizeof (*(Stack))); \
673 Stack = &yyptr->Stack_alloc; \
674 yynewbytes = yystacksize * sizeof (*Stack) + YYSTACK_GAP_MAXIMUM(sizeof (union yyalloc) - 1); \
675 yyptr += yynewbytes / sizeof (*yyptr); \
676 } \
677 while (YYID (0)(0))
678
679#endif
680
681#if defined YYCOPY_NEEDED1 && YYCOPY_NEEDED1
682/* Copy COUNT objects from SRC to DST. The source and destination do
683 not overlap. */
684# ifndef YYCOPY
685# if defined __GNUC__4 && 1 < __GNUC__4
686# define YYCOPY(Dst, Src, Count)__builtin_memcpy (Dst, Src, (Count) * sizeof (*(Src))) \
687 __builtin_memcpy (Dst, Src, (Count) * sizeof (*(Src)))
688# else
689# define YYCOPY(Dst, Src, Count)__builtin_memcpy (Dst, Src, (Count) * sizeof (*(Src))) \
690 do \
691 { \
692 YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int yyi; \
693 for (yyi = 0; yyi < (Count); yyi++) \
694 (Dst)[yyi] = (Src)[yyi]; \
695 } \
696 while (YYID (0)(0))
697# endif
698# endif
699#endif /* !YYCOPY_NEEDED */

yyssp; goto yybackup; } else { parser_error ("syntax error: cannot back up"
); goto yyerrorlab; } while ((0)) \

2306
2307# ifndef yystrlenstrlen
2308# if defined __GLIBC__2 && defined _STRING_H1
2309# define yystrlenstrlen strlen
2310# else
2311/* Return the length of YYSTR. */
2312#if (defined __STDC__1 || defined __C99__FUNC__ \
2313 || defined __cplusplus || defined _MSC_VER)
2314static YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int
2315yystrlenstrlen (const char *yystr)
2316#else
2317static YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int
2318yystrlenstrlen (yystr)
2319 const char *yystr;
2320#endif
2321{
2322 YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int yylen;
2323 for (yylen = 0; yystr[yylen]; yylen++)
2324 continue;
2325 return yylen;

2330# ifndef yystpcpy
2331# if defined __GLIBC__2 && defined _STRING_H1 && defined _GNU_SOURCE
2332# define yystpcpy stpcpy
2333# else
2334/* Copy YYSRC to YYDEST, returning the address of the terminating '\0' in
2335 YYDEST. */
2336#if (defined __STDC__1 || defined __C99__FUNC__ \
2337 || defined __cplusplus || defined _MSC_VER)
2338static char *
2339yystpcpy (char *yydest, const char *yysrc)
2340#else
2341static char *
2342yystpcpy (yydest, yysrc)
2343 char *yydest;
2344 const char *yysrc;
2345#endif
2346{
2347 char *yyd = yydest;
2348 const char *yys = yysrc;
2349
2350 while ((*yyd++ = *yys++) != '\0')
2351 continue;
2352
2353 return yyd - 1;
2354}
2355# endif
2356# endif
2357
2358# ifndef yytnamerr
2359/* Copy to YYRES the contents of YYSTR after stripping away unnecessary
2360 quotes and backslashes, so that it's suitable for yyerror. The
2361 heuristic is that double-quoting is unnecessary unless the string
2362 contains an apostrophe, a comma, or backslash (other than
2363 backslash-backslash). YYSTR is taken from yytname. If YYRES is
2364 null, do not copy; instead, return the length of what the result
2365 would have been. */
2366static YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int
2367yytnamerr (char *yyres, const char *yystr)
2368{
2369 if (*yystr == '"')
2370 {
2371 YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int yyn = 0;
2372 char const *yyp = yystr;
2373
2374 for (;;)
2375 switch (*++yyp)
2376 {
2377 case '\'':
2378 case ',':
2379 goto do_not_strip_quotes;
2380
2381 case '\\':
2382 if (*++yyp != '\\')
2383 goto do_not_strip_quotes;
2384 /* Fall through. */
2385 default:
2386 if (yyres)
2387 yyres[yyn] = *yyp;
2388 yyn++;
2389 break;
2390
2391 case '"':
2392 if (yyres)
2393 yyres[yyn] = '\0';
2394 return yyn;
2395 }
2396 do_not_strip_quotes: ;
2397 }
2398
2399 if (! yyres)
2400 return yystrlenstrlen (yystr);
2401
2402 return yystpcpy (yyres, yystr) - yyres;
2403}
2404# endif
2405
2406/* Copy into *YYMSG, which is of size *YYMSG_ALLOC, an error message
2407 about the unexpected token YYTOKEN for the state stack whose top is
2408 YYSSP.
2409
2410 Return 0 if *YYMSG was successfully written. Return 1 if *YYMSG is
2411 not large enough to hold the message. In that case, also set
2412 *YYMSG_ALLOC to the required number of bytes. Return 2 if the
2413 required number of bytes is too large to store. */
2414static int
2415yysyntax_error (YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int *yymsg_alloc, char **yymsg,
2416 yytype_int16 *yyssp, int yytoken)
2417{
2418 YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int yysize0 = yytnamerr (YY_NULL0, yytname[yytoken]);
2419 YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int yysize = yysize0;
2420 enum { YYERROR_VERBOSE_ARGS_MAXIMUM = 5 };
2421 /* Internationalized format string. */
2422 const char *yyformat = YY_NULL0;
2423 /* Arguments of yyformat. */
2424 char const *yyarg[YYERROR_VERBOSE_ARGS_MAXIMUM];
2425 /* Number of reported tokens (one for the "unexpected", one per
2426 "expected"). */
2427 int yycount = 0;
2428
2429 /* There are many possibilities here to consider:
2430 - Assume YYFAIL is not used. It's too flawed to consider. See
2431 <http://lists.gnu.org/archive/html/bison-patches/2009-12/msg00024.html>
2432 for details. YYERROR is fine as it does not invoke this
2433 function.
2434 - If this state is a consistent state with a default action, then
2435 the only way this function was invoked is if the default action
2436 is an error action. In that case, don't check for expected
2437 tokens because there are none.
2438 - The only way there can be no lookahead present (in yychar) is if
2439 this state is a consistent state with a default action. Thus,
2440 detecting the absence of a lookahead is sufficient to determine
2441 that there is no unexpected or expected token to report. In that
2442 case, just report a simple "syntax error".
2443 - Don't assume there isn't a lookahead just because this state is a
2444 consistent state with a default action. There might have been a
2445 previous inconsistent state, consistent state with a non-default
2446 action, or user semantic action that manipulated yychar.
2447 - Of course, the expected token list depends on states to have
2448 correct lookahead information, and it depends on the parser not
2449 to perform extra reductions after fetching a lookahead from the
2450 scanner and before detecting a syntax error. Thus, state merging
2451 (from LALR or IELR) and default reductions corrupt the expected
2452 token list. However, the list is correct for canonical LR with
2453 one exception: it will still contain any token that will not be
2454 accepted due to an error action in a later state.
2455 */
2456 if (yytoken != YYEMPTY(-2))
2457 {
2458 int yyn = yypact[*yyssp];
2459 yyarg[yycount++] = yytname[yytoken];
2460 if (!yypact_value_is_default (yyn)(!!((yyn) == (-526))))
2461 {
2462 /* Start YYX at -YYN if negative to avoid negative indexes in
2463 YYCHECK. In other words, skip the first -YYN actions for
2464 this state because they are default actions. */
2465 int yyxbegin = yyn < 0 ? -yyn : 0;
2466 /* Stay within bounds of both yycheck and yytname. */
2467 int yychecklim = YYLAST3077 - yyn + 1;
2468 int yyxend = yychecklim < YYNTOKENS210 ? yychecklim : YYNTOKENS210;
2469 int yyx;
2470
2471 for (yyx = yyxbegin; yyx < yyxend; ++yyx)
2472 if (yycheck[yyx + yyn] == yyx && yyx != YYTERROR1
2473 && !yytable_value_is_error (yytable[yyx + yyn])(0))
2474 {
2475 if (yycount == YYERROR_VERBOSE_ARGS_MAXIMUM)
2476 {
2477 yycount = 1;
2478 yysize = yysize0;
2479 break;
2480 }
2481 yyarg[yycount++] = yytname[yyx];
2482 {
2483 YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int yysize1 = yysize + yytnamerr (YY_NULL0, yytname[yyx]);
2484 if (! (yysize <= yysize1
2485 && yysize1 <= YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM((long unsigned int) -1)))
2486 return 2;
2487 yysize = yysize1;
2488 }
2489 }
2490 }
2491 }
2492
2493 switch (yycount)
2494 {
2495# define YYCASE_(N, S) \
2496 case N: \
2497 yyformat = S; \
2498 break
2499 YYCASE_(0, YY_("syntax error")"syntax error");
2500 YYCASE_(1, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s")"syntax error, unexpected %s");
2501 YYCASE_(2, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s")"syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s");
2502 YYCASE_(3, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s")"syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s");
2503 YYCASE_(4, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s or %s")"syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s or %s");
2504 YYCASE_(5, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s or %s or %s")"syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s or %s or %s");
2505# undef YYCASE_
2506 }
2507
2508 {
2509 YYSIZE_Tlong unsigned int yysize1 = yysize + yystrlenstrlen (yyformat);
2510 if (! (yysize <= yysize1 && yysize1 <= YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM((long unsigned int) -1)))
2511 return 2;
2512 yysize = yysize1;
2513 }
2514
2515 if (*yymsg_alloc < yysize)
2516 {
2517 *yymsg_alloc = 2 * yysize;
2518 if (! (yysize <= *yymsg_alloc
2519 && *yymsg_alloc <= YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM((long unsigned int) -1)))
2520 *yymsg_alloc = YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM((long unsigned int) -1);
2521 return 1;
2522 }
2523
2524 /* Avoid sprintf, as that infringes on the user's name space.
2525 Don't have undefined behavior even if the translation
2526 produced a string with the wrong number of "%s"s. */
2527 {
2528 char *yyp = *yymsg;
2529 int yyi = 0;
2530 while ((*yyp = *yyformat) != '\0')
2531 if (*yyp == '%' && yyformat[1] == 's' && yyi < yycount)
2532 {

5461static str_list_t *append_str(str_list_t *list, char *str)
5462{
5463 struct str_list_entry_t *entry;
5464
5465 if (!str) return list;
5466 if (!list)
5467 {
5468 list = xmalloc( sizeof(*list) );
5469 list_init( list );
5470 }
5471 entry = xmalloc( sizeof(*entry) );
5472 entry->str = str;
5473 list_add_tail( list, &entry->entry );
5474 return list;
5475}

5477static attr_list_t *append_attr(attr_list_t *list, attr_t *attr)
5478{
5479 attr_t *attr_existing;
5480 if (!attr) return list;
5481 if (!list)
5482 {
5483 list = xmalloc( sizeof(*list) );
5484 list_init( list );
5485 }
5486 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(attr_existing, list, attr_t, entry)for ((attr_existing) = ((attr_t *)((char *)((list)->next) -
__builtin_offsetof(attr_t, entry))); &(attr_existing)->
entry != (list); (attr_existing) = ((attr_t *)((char *)((attr_existing
)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof(attr_t, entry))))
5487 if (attr_existing->type == attr->type)
5488 {
5489 parser_warning("duplicate attribute %s\n", get_attr_display_name(attr->type));
5490 /* use the last attribute, like MIDL does */
5491 list_remove(&attr_existing->entry);
5492 break;
5493 }
5494 list_add_tail( list, &attr->entry );
5495 return list;
5496}

5498static attr_list_t *move_attr(attr_list_t *dst, attr_list_t *src, enum attr_type type)
5499{
5500 attr_t *attr;
5501 if (!src) return dst;
5502 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(attr, src, attr_t, entry)for ((attr) = ((attr_t *)((char *)((src)->next) - __builtin_offsetof
(attr_t, entry))); &(attr)->entry != (src); (attr) = (
(attr_t *)((char *)((attr)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof
(attr_t, entry))))
5503 if (attr->type == type)
5504 {
5505 list_remove(&attr->entry);
5506 return append_attr(dst, attr);
5507 }
5508 return dst;
5509}
5510
5511static attr_list_t *append_attr_list(attr_list_t *new_list, attr_list_t *old_list)
5512{
5513 struct list *entry;
5514
5515 if (!old_list) return new_list;
5516
5517 while ((entry = list_head(old_list)))
5518 {
5519 attr_t *attr = LIST_ENTRY(entry, attr_t, entry)((attr_t *)((char *)(entry) - __builtin_offsetof(attr_t, entry
)));
5520 list_remove(entry);
5521 new_list = append_attr(new_list, attr);
5522 }
5523 return new_list;
5524}
5525
5526static attr_list_t *dupattrs(const attr_list_t *list)
5527{
5528 attr_list_t *new_list;
5529 const attr_t *attr;
5530
5531 if (!list) return NULL((void*)0);
5532
5533 new_list = xmalloc( sizeof(*list) );
5534 list_init( new_list );
5535 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(attr, list, const attr_t, entry)for ((attr) = ((const attr_t *)((char *)((list)->next) - __builtin_offsetof
(const attr_t, entry))); &(attr)->entry != (list); (attr
) = ((const attr_t *)((char *)((attr)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof
(const attr_t, entry))))
5536 {
5537 attr_t *new_attr = xmalloc(sizeof(*new_attr));
5538 *new_attr = *attr;
5539 list_add_tail(new_list, &new_attr->entry);
5540 }
5541 return new_list;
5542}
5543
5544static decl_spec_t *make_decl_spec(type_t *type, decl_spec_t *left, decl_spec_t *right, attr_t *attr, enum storage_class stgclass)
5545{
5546 decl_spec_t *declspec = left ? left : right;
5547 if (!declspec)
5548 {
5549 declspec = xmalloc(sizeof(*declspec));
5550 declspec->type = NULL((void*)0);
5551 declspec->attrs = NULL((void*)0);
5552 declspec->stgclass = STG_NONE;
5553 }
5554 declspec->type = type;
5555 if (left && declspec != left)
5556 {
5557 declspec->attrs = append_attr_list(declspec->attrs, left->attrs);
5558 if (declspec->stgclass == STG_NONE)
5559 declspec->stgclass = left->stgclass;
5560 else if (left->stgclass != STG_NONE)
5561 error_loc("only one storage class can be specified\n");
5562 assert(!left->type)((!left->type) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail ("!left->type"
, "parser.y", 1245, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
5563 free(left);
5564 }
5565 if (right && declspec != right)
5566 {
5567 declspec->attrs = append_attr_list(declspec->attrs, right->attrs);
5568 if (declspec->stgclass == STG_NONE)
5569 declspec->stgclass = right->stgclass;
5570 else if (right->stgclass != STG_NONE)
5571 error_loc("only one storage class can be specified\n");
5572 assert(!right->type)((!right->type) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail ("!right->type"
, "parser.y", 1255, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
5573 free(right);
5574 }
5575
5576 declspec->attrs = append_attr(declspec->attrs, attr);
5577 if (declspec->stgclass == STG_NONE)
5578 declspec->stgclass = stgclass;
5579 else if (stgclass != STG_NONE)
5580 error_loc("only one storage class can be specified\n");
5581
5582 /* apply attributes to type */
5583 if (type && declspec->attrs)
5584 {
5585 attr_list_t *attrs;
5586 declspec->type = duptype(type, 1);
5587 attrs = dupattrs(type->attrs);
5588 declspec->type->attrs = append_attr_list(attrs, declspec->attrs);
5589 declspec->attrs = NULL((void*)0);
5590 }
5591
5592 return declspec;
5593}

5598 a->type = type;

5600 return a;
5601}

5643static struct list type_pool = LIST_INIT(type_pool){ &(type_pool), &(type_pool) };
5644typedef struct
5645{
5646 type_t data;
5647 struct list link;
5648} type_pool_node_t;
5649
5650type_t *alloc_type(void)
5651{
5652 type_pool_node_t *node = xmalloc(sizeof *node);
5653 list_add_tail(&type_pool, &node->link);
5654 return &node->data;
5655}
5656
5657void set_all_tfswrite(int val)
5658{
5659 type_pool_node_t *node;
5660 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(node, &type_pool, type_pool_node_t, link)for ((node) = ((type_pool_node_t *)((char *)((&type_pool)
->next) - __builtin_offsetof(type_pool_node_t, link))); &
(node)->link != (&type_pool); (node) = ((type_pool_node_t
*)((char *)((node)->link.next) - __builtin_offsetof(type_pool_node_t
, link))))
5661 node->data.tfswrite = val;
5662}
5663
5664void clear_all_offsets(void)
5665{
5666 type_pool_node_t *node;
5667 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(node, &type_pool, type_pool_node_t, link)for ((node) = ((type_pool_node_t *)((char *)((&type_pool)
->next) - __builtin_offsetof(type_pool_node_t, link))); &
(node)->link != (&type_pool); (node) = ((type_pool_node_t
*)((char *)((node)->link.next) - __builtin_offsetof(type_pool_node_t
, link))))
5668 node->data.typestring_offset = node->data.ptrdesc = 0;
5669}

5671static void type_function_add_head_arg(type_t *type, var_t *arg)
5672{

5674 {
5675 type->details.function->args = xmalloc( sizeof(*type->details.function->args) );
5676 list_init( type->details.function->args );
5677 }
5678 list_add_head( type->details.function->args, &arg->entry );

5680
5681static int is_allowed_range_type(const type_t *type)
5682{
5683 switch (type_get_type(type))
5684 {
5685 case TYPE_ENUM:
5686 return TRUE1;
5687 case TYPE_BASIC:
5688 switch (type_basic_get_type(type))
5689 {
5690 case TYPE_BASIC_INT8:
5691 case TYPE_BASIC_INT16:
5692 case TYPE_BASIC_INT32:
5693 case TYPE_BASIC_INT64:
5694 case TYPE_BASIC_INT:
5695 case TYPE_BASIC_INT3264:
5696 case TYPE_BASIC_BYTE:
5697 case TYPE_BASIC_CHAR:
5698 case TYPE_BASIC_WCHAR:
5699 case TYPE_BASIC_HYPER:
5700 return TRUE1;
5701 case TYPE_BASIC_FLOAT:
5702 case TYPE_BASIC_DOUBLE:
5703 case TYPE_BASIC_ERROR_STATUS_T:
5704 case TYPE_BASIC_HANDLE:
5705 return FALSE0;
5706 }
5707 return FALSE0;
5708 default:
5709 return FALSE0;
5710 }
5711}
5712
5713static type_t *append_ptrchain_type(type_t *ptrchain, type_t *type)
5714{
5715 type_t *ptrchain_type;
5716 if (!ptrchain)
5717 return type;
5718 for (ptrchain_type = ptrchain; type_pointer_get_ref(ptrchain_type); ptrchain_type = type_pointer_get_ref(ptrchain_type))
5719 ;
5720 assert(ptrchain_type->type_type == TYPE_POINTER)((ptrchain_type->type_type == TYPE_POINTER) ? (void) (0) :
__assert_fail ("ptrchain_type->type_type == TYPE_POINTER"
, "parser.y", 1403, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
5721 ptrchain_type->details.pointer.ref = type;
5722 return ptrchain;
5723}
5724
5725static var_t *declare_var(attr_list_t *attrs, decl_spec_t *decl_spec, const declarator_t *decl,
5726 int top)
5727{
5728 var_t *v = decl->var;
5729 expr_list_t *sizes = get_attrp(attrs, ATTR_SIZEIS);
5730 expr_list_t *lengs = get_attrp(attrs, ATTR_LENGTHIS);
5731 int sizeless;
5732 expr_t *dim;
5733 type_t **ptype;
5734 array_dims_t *arr = decl ? decl->array : NULL((void*)0);
5735 type_t *func_type = decl ? decl->func_type : NULL((void*)0);
5736 type_t *type = decl_spec->type;
5737
5738 if (is_attr(type->attrs, ATTR_INLINE))
5739 {
5740 if (!func_type)
5741 error_loc("inline attribute applied to non-function type\n");
5742 else
5743 {
5744 type_t *t;
5745 /* move inline attribute from return type node to function node */
5746 for (t = func_type; is_ptr(t); t = type_pointer_get_ref(t))
5747 ;
5748 t->attrs = move_attr(t->attrs, type->attrs, ATTR_INLINE);
5749 }
5750 }
5751
5752 /* add type onto the end of the pointers in pident->type */
5753 v->type = append_ptrchain_type(decl ? decl->type : NULL((void*)0), type);
5754 v->stgclass = decl_spec->stgclass;
5755 v->attrs = attrs;
5756
5757 /* check for pointer attribute being applied to non-pointer, non-array
5758 * type */
5759 if (!arr)
5760 {
5761 int ptr_attr = get_attrv(v->attrs, ATTR_POINTERTYPE);
5762 const type_t *ptr = NULL((void*)0);
5763 /* pointer attributes on the left side of the type belong to the function
5764 * pointer, if one is being declared */
5765 type_t **pt = func_type ? &func_type : &v->type;
5766 for (ptr = *pt; ptr && !ptr_attr; )
5767 {
5768 ptr_attr = get_attrv(ptr->attrs, ATTR_POINTERTYPE);
5769 if (!ptr_attr && type_is_alias(ptr))
5770 ptr = type_alias_get_aliasee(ptr);
5771 else
5772 break;
5773 }
5774 if (is_ptr(ptr))
5775 {
5776 if (ptr_attr && ptr_attr != RPC_FC_UP0x12 &&
5777 type_get_type(type_pointer_get_ref(ptr)) == TYPE_INTERFACE)
5778 warning_loc_info(&v->loc_info,
5779 "%s: pointer attribute applied to interface "
5780 "pointer type has no effect\n", v->name);
5781 if (!ptr_attr && top && (*pt)->details.pointer.def_fc != RPC_FC_RP0x11)
5782 {
5783 /* FIXME: this is a horrible hack to cope with the issue that we
5784 * store an offset to the typeformat string in the type object, but
5785 * two typeformat strings may be written depending on whether the
5786 * pointer is a toplevel parameter or not */
5787 *pt = duptype(*pt, 1);
5788 }
5789 }
5790 else if (ptr_attr)
5791 error_loc("%s: pointer attribute applied to non-pointer type\n", v->name);
5792 }
5793
5794 if (is_attr(v->attrs, ATTR_STRING))
5795 {
5796 type_t *t = type;
5797
5798 if (!is_ptr(v->type) && !arr)
5799 error_loc("'%s': [string] attribute applied to non-pointer, non-array type\n",
5800 v->name);
5801
5802 while (is_ptr(t))
5803 t = type_pointer_get_ref(t);
5804
5805 if (type_get_type(t) != TYPE_BASIC &&
5806 (get_basic_fc(t) != RPC_FC_CHAR0x02 &&
5807 get_basic_fc(t) != RPC_FC_BYTE0x01 &&
5808 get_basic_fc(t) != RPC_FC_WCHAR0x05))
5809 {
5810 error_loc("'%s': [string] attribute is only valid on 'char', 'byte', or 'wchar_t' pointers and arrays\n",
5811 v->name);
5812 }
5813 }
5814
5815 if (is_attr(v->attrs, ATTR_V1ENUM))
5816 {
5817 if (type_get_type_detect_alias(v->type) != TYPE_ENUM)
5818 error_loc("'%s': [v1_enum] attribute applied to non-enum type\n", v->name);
5819 }
5820
5821 if (is_attr(v->attrs, ATTR_RANGE) && !is_allowed_range_type(v->type))
5822 error_loc("'%s': [range] attribute applied to non-integer type\n",
5823 v->name);
5824
5825 ptype = &v->type;
5826 sizeless = FALSE0;
5827 if (arr) LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY_REV(dim, arr, expr_t, entry)for ((dim) = ((expr_t *)((char *)((arr)->prev) - __builtin_offsetof
(expr_t, entry))); &(dim)->entry != (arr); (dim) = ((expr_t
*)((char *)((dim)->entry.prev) - __builtin_offsetof(expr_t
, entry))))
5828 {
5829 if (sizeless)
5830 error_loc("%s: only the first array dimension can be unspecified\n", v->name);
5831
5832 if (dim->is_const)
5833 {
5834 if (dim->cval <= 0)
5835 error_loc("%s: array dimension must be positive\n", v->name);
5836
5837 /* FIXME: should use a type_memsize that allows us to pass in a pointer size */
5838 if (0)
5839 {
5840 unsigned int size = type_memsize(v->type);
5841
5842 if (0xffffffffu / size < dim->cval)
5843 error_loc("%s: total array size is too large\n", v->name);
5844 }
5845 }
5846 else
5847 sizeless = TRUE1;
5848
5849 *ptype = type_new_array(NULL((void*)0), *ptype, FALSE0,
5850 dim->is_const ? dim->cval : 0,
5851 dim->is_const ? NULL((void*)0) : dim, NULL((void*)0),
5852 pointer_default);
5853 }
5854
5855 ptype = &v->type;
5856 if (sizes) LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(dim, sizes, expr_t, entry)for ((dim) = ((expr_t *)((char *)((sizes)->next) - __builtin_offsetof
(expr_t, entry))); &(dim)->entry != (sizes); (dim) = (
(expr_t *)((char *)((dim)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof
(expr_t, entry))))
5857 {
5858 if (dim->type != EXPR_VOID)
5859 {
5860 if (is_array(*ptype))
5861 {
5862 if (!type_array_get_conformance(*ptype) ||
5863 type_array_get_conformance(*ptype)->type != EXPR_VOID)
5864 error_loc("%s: cannot specify size_is for an already sized array\n", v->name);
5865 else
5866 *ptype = type_new_array((*ptype)->name,
5867 type_array_get_element(*ptype), FALSE0,
5868 0, dim, NULL((void*)0), 0);
5869 }
5870 else if (is_ptr(*ptype))
5871 *ptype = type_new_array((*ptype)->name, type_pointer_get_ref(*ptype), TRUE1,
5872 0, dim, NULL((void*)0), pointer_default);
5873 else
5874 error_loc("%s: size_is attribute applied to illegal type\n", v->name);
5875 }
5876
5877 if (is_ptr(*ptype))
5878 ptype = &(*ptype)->details.pointer.ref;
5879 else if (is_array(*ptype))
5880 ptype = &(*ptype)->details.array.elem;
5881 else
5882 error_loc("%s: too many expressions in size_is attribute\n", v->name);
5883 }
5884
5885 ptype = &v->type;
5886 if (lengs) LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(dim, lengs, expr_t, entry)for ((dim) = ((expr_t *)((char *)((lengs)->next) - __builtin_offsetof
(expr_t, entry))); &(dim)->entry != (lengs); (dim) = (
(expr_t *)((char *)((dim)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof
(expr_t, entry))))
5887 {
5888 if (dim->type != EXPR_VOID)
5889 {
5890 if (is_array(*ptype))
5891 {
5892 *ptype = type_new_array((*ptype)->name,
5893 type_array_get_element(*ptype),
5894 type_array_is_decl_as_ptr(*ptype),
5895 type_array_get_dim(*ptype),
5896 type_array_get_conformance(*ptype),
5897 dim, type_array_get_ptr_default_fc(*ptype));
5898 }
5899 else
5900 error_loc("%s: length_is attribute applied to illegal type\n", v->name);
5901 }
5902
5903 if (is_ptr(*ptype))
5904 ptype = &(*ptype)->details.pointer.ref;
5905 else if (is_array(*ptype))
5906 ptype = &(*ptype)->details.array.elem;
5907 else
5908 error_loc("%s: too many expressions in length_is attribute\n", v->name);
5909 }
5910
5911 /* v->type is currently pointing to the type on the left-side of the
5912 * declaration, so we need to fix this up so that it is the return type of the
5913 * function and make v->type point to the function side of the declaration */
5914 if (func_type)
5915 {
5916 type_t *ft, *t;
5917 type_t *return_type = v->type;
5918 v->type = func_type;
5919 for (ft = v->type; is_ptr(ft); ft = type_pointer_get_ref(ft))
5920 ;
5921 assert(type_get_type_detect_alias(ft) == TYPE_FUNCTION)((type_get_type_detect_alias(ft) == TYPE_FUNCTION) ? (void) (
0) : __assert_fail ("type_get_type_detect_alias(ft) == TYPE_FUNCTION"
, "parser.y", 1604, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
5922 ft->details.function->retval = make_var(xstrdup("_RetVal"));
5923 ft->details.function->retval->type = return_type;
5924 /* move calling convention attribute, if present, from pointer nodes to
5925 * function node */
5926 for (t = v->type; is_ptr(t); t = type_pointer_get_ref(t))
5927 ft->attrs = move_attr(ft->attrs, t->attrs, ATTR_CALLCONV);
5928 }
5929 else
5930 {
5931 type_t *t;
5932 for (t = v->type; is_ptr(t); t = type_pointer_get_ref(t))
5933 if (is_attr(t->attrs, ATTR_CALLCONV))
5934 error_loc("calling convention applied to non-function-pointer type\n");
5935 }
5936
5937 if (decl->bits)
5938 v->type = type_new_bitfield(v->type, decl->bits);
5939
5940 return v;
5941}
5942
5943static var_list_t *set_var_types(attr_list_t *attrs, decl_spec_t *decl_spec, declarator_list_t *decls)
5944{
5945 declarator_t *decl, *next;
5946 var_list_t *var_list = NULL((void*)0);
5947
5948 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY_SAFE( decl, next, decls, declarator_t, entry )for ((decl) = ((declarator_t *)((char *)((decls)->next) - __builtin_offsetof
(declarator_t, entry))), (next) = ((declarator_t *)((char *)(
(decl)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof(declarator_t, entry
))); &(decl)->entry != (decls); (decl) = (next), (next
) = ((declarator_t *)((char *)((decl)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof
(declarator_t, entry))))
5949 {
5950 var_t *var = declare_var(attrs, decl_spec, decl, 0);
5951 var_list = append_var(var_list, var);
5952 free(decl);
5953 }
5954 free(decl_spec);
5955 return var_list;
5956}

6050
6051#define HASHMAX64 64
6052
6053static int hash_ident(const char *name)
6054{
6055 const char *p = name;
6056 int sum = 0;
6057 /* a simple sum hash is probably good enough */
6058 while (*p) {
6059 sum += *p;
6060 p++;
6061 }
6062 return sum & (HASHMAX64-1);
6063}
6064
6065/***** type repository *****/
6066
6067struct rtype {
6068 const char *name;
6069 type_t *type;
6070 int t;
6071 struct rtype *next;
6072};
6073
6074struct rtype *type_hash[HASHMAX64];
6075
6076type_t *reg_type(type_t *type, const char *name, int t)
6077{
6078 struct rtype *nt;
6079 int hash;
6080 if (!name) {
6081 error_loc("registering named type without name\n");
6082 return type;
6083 }
6084 hash = hash_ident(name);
6085 nt = xmalloc(sizeof(struct rtype));
6086 nt->name = name;
6087 nt->type = type;
6088 nt->t = t;
6089 nt->next = type_hash[hash];
6090 type_hash[hash] = nt;
6091 if ((t == tsSTRUCT2 || t == tsUNION3))
6092 fix_incomplete_types(type);
6093 return type;
6094}
6095
6096static int is_incomplete(const type_t *t)
6097{
6098 return !t->defined &&
6099 (type_get_type_detect_alias(t) == TYPE_STRUCT ||
6100 type_get_type_detect_alias(t) == TYPE_UNION ||
6101 type_get_type_detect_alias(t) == TYPE_ENCAPSULATED_UNION);
6102}
6103
6104void add_incomplete(type_t *t)
6105{
6106 struct typenode *tn = xmalloc(sizeof *tn);
6107 tn->type = t;
6108 list_add_tail(&incomplete_types, &tn->entry);
6109}
6110
6111static void fix_type(type_t *t)
6112{
6113 if (type_is_alias(t) && is_incomplete(t)) {
6114 type_t *ot = type_alias_get_aliasee(t);
6115 fix_type(ot);
6116 if (type_get_type_detect_alias(ot) == TYPE_STRUCT ||
6117 type_get_type_detect_alias(ot) == TYPE_UNION ||
6118 type_get_type_detect_alias(ot) == TYPE_ENCAPSULATED_UNION)
6119 t->details.structure = ot->details.structure;
6120 t->defined = ot->defined;
6121 }
6122}
6123
6124static void fix_incomplete(void)
6125{
6126 struct typenode *tn, *next;
6127
6128 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY_SAFE(tn, next, &incomplete_types, struct typenode, entry)for ((tn) = ((struct typenode *)((char *)((&incomplete_types
)->next) - __builtin_offsetof(struct typenode, entry))), (
next) = ((struct typenode *)((char *)((tn)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof
(struct typenode, entry))); &(tn)->entry != (&incomplete_types
); (tn) = (next), (next) = ((struct typenode *)((char *)((tn)
->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof(struct typenode, entry)
))) {
6129 fix_type(tn->type);
6130 list_remove(&tn->entry);
6131 free(tn);
6132 }
6133}
6134
6135static void fix_incomplete_types(type_t *complete_type)
6136{
6137 struct typenode *tn, *next;
6138
6139 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY_SAFE(tn, next, &incomplete_types, struct typenode, entry)for ((tn) = ((struct typenode *)((char *)((&incomplete_types
)->next) - __builtin_offsetof(struct typenode, entry))), (
next) = ((struct typenode *)((char *)((tn)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof
(struct typenode, entry))); &(tn)->entry != (&incomplete_types
); (tn) = (next), (next) = ((struct typenode *)((char *)((tn)
->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof(struct typenode, entry)
)))
6140 {
6141 if (type_is_equal(complete_type, tn->type))
6142 {
6143 tn->type->details.structure = complete_type->details.structure;
6144 list_remove(&tn->entry);
6145 free(tn);
6146 }
6147 }
6148}
6149
6150static type_t *reg_typedefs(decl_spec_t *decl_spec, declarator_list_t *decls, attr_list_t *attrs)
6151{
6152 const declarator_t *decl;
6153 type_t *type = decl_spec->type;
6154
6155 /* We must generate names for tagless enum, struct or union.
6156 Typedef-ing a tagless enum, struct or union means we want the typedef
6157 to be included in a library hence the public attribute. */
6158 if ((type_get_type_detect_alias(type) == TYPE_ENUM ||
6159 type_get_type_detect_alias(type) == TYPE_STRUCT ||
6160 type_get_type_detect_alias(type) == TYPE_UNION ||
6161 type_get_type_detect_alias(type) == TYPE_ENCAPSULATED_UNION) &&
6162 !type->name)
6163 {
6164 if (! is_attr(attrs, ATTR_PUBLIC) && ! is_attr (attrs, ATTR_HIDDEN))
6165 attrs = append_attr( attrs, make_attr(ATTR_PUBLIC) );
6166 type->name = gen_name();
6167 }
6168 else if (is_attr(attrs, ATTR_UUID) && !is_attr(attrs, ATTR_PUBLIC)
6169 && !is_attr(attrs, ATTR_HIDDEN))
6170 attrs = append_attr( attrs, make_attr(ATTR_PUBLIC) );
6171
6172 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY( decl, decls, const declarator_t, entry )for ((decl) = ((const declarator_t *)((char *)((decls)->next
) - __builtin_offsetof(const declarator_t, entry))); &(decl
)->entry != (decls); (decl) = ((const declarator_t *)((char
*)((decl)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof(const declarator_t
, entry))))
6173 {
6174
6175 if (decl->var->name) {
6176 type_t *cur;
6177 var_t *name;
6178
6179 cur = find_type(decl->var->name, 0);
6180
6181 /*
6182 * MIDL allows shadowing types that are declared in imported files.
6183 * We don't throw an error in this case and instead add a new type
6184 * (which is earlier on the list in hash table, so it will be used
6185 * instead of shadowed type).
6186 *
6187 * FIXME: We may consider string separated type tables for each input
6188 * for cleaner solution.
6189 */
6190 if (cur && input_name == cur->loc_info.input_name)
6191 error_loc("%s: redefinition error; original definition was at %s:%d\n",
6192 cur->name, cur->loc_info.input_name,
6193 cur->loc_info.line_number);
6194
6195 name = declare_var(attrs, decl_spec, decl, 0);
6196 cur = type_new_alias(name->type, name->name);
6197 cur->attrs = attrs;
6198
6199 if (is_incomplete(cur))
6200 add_incomplete(cur);
6201 reg_type(cur, cur->name, 0);
6202 }
6203 }
6204 return type;
6205}
6206
6207type_t *find_type(const char *name, int t)
6208{
6209 struct rtype *cur = type_hash[hash_ident(name)];
6210 while (cur && (cur->t != t || strcmp(cur->name, name)__extension__ ({ size_t __s1_len, __s2_len; (__builtin_constant_p
(cur->name) && __builtin_constant_p (name) &&
(__s1_len = strlen (cur->name), __s2_len = strlen (name),
(!((size_t)(const void *)((cur->name) + 1) - (size_t)(const
void *)(cur->name) == 1) || __s1_len >= 4) && (
!((size_t)(const void *)((name) + 1) - (size_t)(const void *)
(name) == 1) || __s2_len >= 4)) ? __builtin_strcmp (cur->
name, name) : (__builtin_constant_p (cur->name) &&
((size_t)(const void *)((cur->name) + 1) - (size_t)(const
void *)(cur->name) == 1) && (__s1_len = strlen (cur
->name), __s1_len < 4) ? (__builtin_constant_p (name) &&
((size_t)(const void *)((name) + 1) - (size_t)(const void *)
(name) == 1) ? __builtin_strcmp (cur->name, name) : (__extension__
({ const unsigned char *__s2 = (const unsigned char *) (const
char *) (name); register int __result = (((const unsigned char
*) (const char *) (cur->name))[0] - __s2[0]); if (__s1_len
> 0 && __result == 0) { __result = (((const unsigned
char *) (const char *) (cur->name))[1] - __s2[1]); if (__s1_len
> 1 && __result == 0) { __result = (((const unsigned
char *) (const char *) (cur->name))[2] - __s2[2]); if (__s1_len
> 2 && __result == 0) __result = (((const unsigned
char *) (const char *) (cur->name))[3] - __s2[3]); } } __result
; }))) : (__builtin_constant_p (name) && ((size_t)(const
void *)((name) + 1) - (size_t)(const void *)(name) == 1) &&
(__s2_len = strlen (name), __s2_len < 4) ? (__builtin_constant_p
(cur->name) && ((size_t)(const void *)((cur->name
) + 1) - (size_t)(const void *)(cur->name) == 1) ? __builtin_strcmp
(cur->name, name) : (__extension__ ({ const unsigned char
*__s1 = (const unsigned char *) (const char *) (cur->name
); register int __result = __s1[0] - ((const unsigned char *)
(const char *) (name))[0]; if (__s2_len > 0 && __result
== 0) { __result = (__s1[1] - ((const unsigned char *) (const

== 0) { __result = (__s1[2] - ((const unsigned char *) (const
char *) (name))[2]); if (__s2_len > 2 && __result
== 0) __result = (__s1[3] - ((const unsigned char *) (const char
*) (name))[3]); } } __result; }))) : __builtin_strcmp (cur->
name, name)))); })))
6211 cur = cur->next;
6212 return cur ? cur->type : NULL((void*)0);
6213}
6214
6215static type_t *find_type_or_error(const char *name, int t)
6216{
6217 type_t *type = find_type(name, t);
6218 if (!type) {
6219 error_loc("type '%s' not found\n", name);
6220 return NULL((void*)0);
6221 }
6222 return type;
6223}
6224
6225static type_t *find_type_or_error2(char *name, int t)
6226{
6227 type_t *tp = find_type_or_error(name, t);
6228 free(name);
6229 return tp;
6230}
6231
6232int is_type(const char *name)
6233{
6234 return find_type(name, 0) != NULL((void*)0);
6235}
6236
6237type_t *get_type(enum type_type type, char *name, int t)
6238{
6239 type_t *tp;
6240 if (name) {
6241 tp = find_type(name, t);
6242 if (tp) {
6243 free(name);
6244 return tp;
6245 }
6246 }
6247 tp = make_type(type);
6248 tp->name = name;
6249 if (!name) return tp;
6250 return reg_type(tp, name, t);
6251}
6252
6253/***** constant repository *****/
6254
6255struct rconst {
6256 char *name;
6257 var_t *var;
6258 struct rconst *next;
6259};
6260
6261struct rconst *const_hash[HASHMAX64];
6262
6263static var_t *reg_const(var_t *var)
6264{
6265 struct rconst *nc;
6266 int hash;
6267 if (!var->name) {
6268 error_loc("registering constant without name\n");
6269 return var;
6270 }
6271 hash = hash_ident(var->name);
6272 nc = xmalloc(sizeof(struct rconst));
6273 nc->name = var->name;
6274 nc->var = var;
6275 nc->next = const_hash[hash];
6276 const_hash[hash] = nc;
6277 return var;
6278}
6279
6280var_t *find_const(const char *name, int f)
6281{

6283 while (cur && strcmp(cur->name, name)__extension__ ({ size_t __s1_len, __s2_len; (__builtin_constant_p
(cur->name) && __builtin_constant_p (name) &&
(__s1_len = strlen (cur->name), __s2_len = strlen (name),
(!((size_t)(const void *)((cur->name) + 1) - (size_t)(const
void *)(cur->name) == 1) || __s1_len >= 4) && (
!((size_t)(const void *)((name) + 1) - (size_t)(const void *)
(name) == 1) || __s2_len >= 4)) ? __builtin_strcmp (cur->
name, name) : (__builtin_constant_p (cur->name) &&
((size_t)(const void *)((cur->name) + 1) - (size_t)(const

->name), __s1_len < 4) ? (__builtin_constant_p (name) &&
((size_t)(const void *)((name) + 1) - (size_t)(const void *)
(name) == 1) ? __builtin_strcmp (cur->name, name) : (__extension__
({ const unsigned char *__s2 = (const unsigned char *) (const
char *) (name); register int __result = (((const unsigned char
*) (const char *) (cur->name))[0] - __s2[0]); if (__s1_len
> 0 && __result == 0) { __result = (((const unsigned

(__s2_len = strlen (name), __s2_len < 4) ? (__builtin_constant_p
(cur->name) && ((size_t)(const void *)((cur->name

6291
6292static char *gen_name(void)
6293{
6294 static const char format[] = "__WIDL_%s_generated_name_%08lX";
6295 static unsigned long n = 0;
6296 static const char *file_id;
6297 static size_t size;
6298 char *name;
6299
6300 if (! file_id)
6301 {
6302 char *dst = dup_basename(input_idl_name, ".idl");
6303 file_id = dst;
6304
6305 for (; *dst; ++dst)
6306 if (! isalnum((unsigned char) *dst)((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) (((unsigned char) *dst))] & (unsigned
short int) _ISalnum))
6307 *dst = '_';
6308
6309 size = sizeof format - 7 + strlen(file_id) + 8;
6310 }
6311
6312 name = xmalloc(size);
6313 sprintf(name, format, file_id, n++);
6314 return name;
6315}

6443{

6446
6447static attr_list_t *check_iface_attrs(const char *name, attr_list_t *attrs)
6448{
6449 const attr_t *attr;
6450 if (!attrs) return attrs;
6451 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(attr, attrs, const attr_t, entry)for ((attr) = ((const attr_t *)((char *)((attrs)->next) - __builtin_offsetof
(const attr_t, entry))); &(attr)->entry != (attrs); (attr
) = ((const attr_t *)((char *)((attr)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof
(const attr_t, entry))))
6452 {
6453 if (!allowed_attr[attr->type].on_interface)
6454 error_loc("inapplicable attribute %s for interface %s\n",
6455 allowed_attr[attr->type].display_name, name);
6456 if (attr->type == ATTR_IMPLICIT_HANDLE)
6457 {
6458 const var_t *var = attr->u.pval;
6459 if (type_get_type( var->type) == TYPE_BASIC &&
6460 type_basic_get_type( var->type ) == TYPE_BASIC_HANDLE)
6461 continue;
6462 if (is_aliaschain_attr( var->type, ATTR_HANDLE ))
6463 continue;
6464 error_loc("attribute %s requires a handle type in interface %s\n",
6465 allowed_attr[attr->type].display_name, name);
6466 }
6467 }
6468 return attrs;
6469}

6489 {
6490 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(attr, arg->attrs, const attr_t, entry)for ((attr) = ((const attr_t *)((char *)((arg->attrs)->
next) - __builtin_offsetof(const attr_t, entry))); &(attr
)->entry != (arg->attrs); (attr) = ((const attr_t *)((char
*)((attr)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof(const attr_t,
entry))))
6491 {
6492 if (!allowed_attr[attr->type].on_arg)
6493 error_loc("inapplicable attribute %s for argument %s\n",

6615
6616static int is_allowed_conf_type(const type_t *type)
6617{
6618 switch (type_get_type(type))
6619 {
6620 case TYPE_ENUM:
6621 return TRUE1;
6622 case TYPE_BASIC:
6623 switch (type_basic_get_type(type))
6624 {
6625 case TYPE_BASIC_INT8:
6626 case TYPE_BASIC_INT16:
6627 case TYPE_BASIC_INT32:
6628 case TYPE_BASIC_INT64:
6629 case TYPE_BASIC_INT:
6630 case TYPE_BASIC_CHAR:
6631 case TYPE_BASIC_HYPER:
6632 case TYPE_BASIC_BYTE:
6633 case TYPE_BASIC_WCHAR:
6634 return TRUE1;
6635 default:
6636 return FALSE0;
6637 }
6638 case TYPE_ALIAS:
6639 /* shouldn't get here because of type_get_type call above */
6640 assert(0)((0) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail ("0", "parser.y", 2323, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
));
6641 /* fall through */
6642 case TYPE_STRUCT:
6643 case TYPE_UNION:
6644 case TYPE_ENCAPSULATED_UNION:
6645 case TYPE_ARRAY:
6646 case TYPE_POINTER:
6647 case TYPE_VOID:
6648 case TYPE_MODULE:
6649 case TYPE_COCLASS:
6650 case TYPE_FUNCTION:
6651 case TYPE_INTERFACE:
6652 case TYPE_BITFIELD:
6653 return FALSE0;
6654 }
6655 return FALSE0;
6656}
6657
6658static int is_ptr_guid_type(const type_t *type)
6659{
6660 /* first, make sure it is a pointer to something */
6661 if (!is_ptr(type)) return FALSE0;
6662
6663 /* second, make sure it is a pointer to something of size sizeof(GUID),
6664 * i.e. 16 bytes */
6665 return (type_memsize(type_pointer_get_ref(type)) == 16);
6666}
6667
6668static void check_conformance_expr_list(const char *attr_name, const var_t *arg, const type_t *container_type, expr_list_t *expr_list)
6669{
6670 expr_t *dim;
6671 struct expr_loc expr_loc;
6672 expr_loc.v = arg;
6673 expr_loc.attr = attr_name;
6674 if (expr_list) LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(dim, expr_list, expr_t, entry)for ((dim) = ((expr_t *)((char *)((expr_list)->next) - __builtin_offsetof
(expr_t, entry))); &(dim)->entry != (expr_list); (dim)
= ((expr_t *)((char *)((dim)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof
(expr_t, entry))))
6675 {
6676 if (dim->type != EXPR_VOID)
6677 {
6678 const type_t *expr_type = expr_resolve_type(&expr_loc, container_type, dim);
6679 if (!is_allowed_conf_type(expr_type))
6680 error_loc_info(&arg->loc_info, "expression must resolve to integral type <= 32bits for attribute %s\n",
6681 attr_name);
6682 }
6683 }
6684}
6685
6686static void check_remoting_fields(const var_t *var, type_t *type);
6687
6688/* checks that properties common to fields and arguments are consistent */
6689static void check_field_common(const type_t *container_type,
6690 const char *container_name, const var_t *arg)
6691{
6692 type_t *type = arg->type;
6693 int more_to_do;
6694 const char *container_type_name;
6695 const char *var_type;
6696
6697 switch (type_get_type(container_type))
6698 {
6699 case TYPE_STRUCT:
6700 container_type_name = "struct";
6701 var_type = "field";
6702 break;
6703 case TYPE_UNION:
6704 container_type_name = "union";
6705 var_type = "arm";
6706 break;
6707 case TYPE_ENCAPSULATED_UNION:
6708 container_type_name = "encapsulated union";
6709 var_type = "arm";
6710 break;
6711 case TYPE_FUNCTION:
6712 container_type_name = "function";
6713 var_type = "parameter";
6714 break;
6715 default:
6716 /* should be no other container types */
6717 assert(0)((0) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail ("0", "parser.y", 2400, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
));
6718 return;
6719 }
6720
6721 if (is_attr(arg->attrs, ATTR_LENGTHIS) &&
6722 (is_attr(arg->attrs, ATTR_STRING) || is_aliaschain_attr(arg->type, ATTR_STRING)))
6723 error_loc_info(&arg->loc_info,
6724 "string and length_is specified for argument %s are mutually exclusive attributes\n",
6725 arg->name);
6726
6727 if (is_attr(arg->attrs, ATTR_SIZEIS))
6728 {
6729 expr_list_t *size_is_exprs = get_attrp(arg->attrs, ATTR_SIZEIS);
6730 check_conformance_expr_list("size_is", arg, container_type, size_is_exprs);
6731 }
6732 if (is_attr(arg->attrs, ATTR_LENGTHIS))
6733 {
6734 expr_list_t *length_is_exprs = get_attrp(arg->attrs, ATTR_LENGTHIS);
6735 check_conformance_expr_list("length_is", arg, container_type, length_is_exprs);
6736 }
6737 if (is_attr(arg->attrs, ATTR_IIDIS))
6738 {
6739 struct expr_loc expr_loc;
6740 expr_t *expr = get_attrp(arg->attrs, ATTR_IIDIS);
6741 if (expr->type != EXPR_VOID)
6742 {
6743 const type_t *expr_type;
6744 expr_loc.v = arg;
6745 expr_loc.attr = "iid_is";
6746 expr_type = expr_resolve_type(&expr_loc, container_type, expr);
6747 if (!expr_type || !is_ptr_guid_type(expr_type))
6748 error_loc_info(&arg->loc_info, "expression must resolve to pointer to GUID type for attribute iid_is\n");
6749 }
6750 }
6751 if (is_attr(arg->attrs, ATTR_SWITCHIS))
6752 {
6753 struct expr_loc expr_loc;
6754 expr_t *expr = get_attrp(arg->attrs, ATTR_SWITCHIS);
6755 if (expr->type != EXPR_VOID)
6756 {
6757 const type_t *expr_type;
6758 expr_loc.v = arg;
6759 expr_loc.attr = "switch_is";
6760 expr_type = expr_resolve_type(&expr_loc, container_type, expr);
6761 if (!expr_type || !is_allowed_conf_type(expr_type))
6762 error_loc_info(&arg->loc_info, "expression must resolve to integral type <= 32bits for attribute %s\n",
6763 expr_loc.attr);
6764 }
6765 }
6766
6767 do
6768 {
6769 more_to_do = FALSE0;
6770
6771 switch (typegen_detect_type(type, arg->attrs, TDT_IGNORE_STRINGS))
6772 {
6773 case TGT_STRUCT:
6774 case TGT_UNION:
6775 check_remoting_fields(arg, type);
6776 break;
6777 case TGT_INVALID:
6778 {
6779 const char *reason = "is invalid";
6780 switch (type_get_type(type))
6781 {
6782 case TYPE_VOID:
6783 reason = "cannot derive from void *";
6784 break;
6785 case TYPE_FUNCTION:
6786 reason = "cannot be a function pointer";
6787 break;
6788 case TYPE_BITFIELD:
6789 reason = "cannot be a bit-field";
6790 break;
6791 case TYPE_COCLASS:
6792 reason = "cannot be a class";
6793 break;
6794 case TYPE_INTERFACE:
6795 reason = "cannot be a non-pointer to an interface";
6796 break;
6797 case TYPE_MODULE:
6798 reason = "cannot be a module";
6799 break;
6800 default:
6801 break;
6802 }
6803 error_loc_info(&arg->loc_info, "%s \'%s\' of %s \'%s\' %s\n",
6804 var_type, arg->name, container_type_name, container_name, reason);
6805 break;
6806 }
6807 case TGT_CTXT_HANDLE:
6808 case TGT_CTXT_HANDLE_POINTER:
6809 if (type_get_type(container_type) != TYPE_FUNCTION)
6810 error_loc_info(&arg->loc_info,
6811 "%s \'%s\' of %s \'%s\' cannot be a context handle\n",
6812 var_type, arg->name, container_type_name,
6813 container_name);
6814 break;
6815 case TGT_STRING:
6816 {
6817 const type_t *t = type;
6818 while (is_ptr(t))
6819 t = type_pointer_get_ref(t);
6820 if (is_aliaschain_attr(t, ATTR_RANGE))
6821 warning_loc_info(&arg->loc_info, "%s: range not verified for a string of ranged types\n", arg->name);
6822 break;
6823 }
6824 case TGT_POINTER:
6825 type = type_pointer_get_ref(type);
6826 more_to_do = TRUE1;
6827 break;
6828 case TGT_ARRAY:
6829 type = type_array_get_element(type);
6830 more_to_do = TRUE1;
6831 break;
6832 case TGT_USER_TYPE:
6833 case TGT_IFACE_POINTER:
6834 case TGT_BASIC:
6835 case TGT_ENUM:
6836 case TGT_RANGE:
6837 /* nothing to do */
6838 break;
6839 }
6840 } while (more_to_do);
6841}
6842
6843static void check_remoting_fields(const var_t *var, type_t *type)
6844{
6845 const var_t *field;
6846 const var_list_t *fields = NULL((void*)0);
6847
6848 type = type_get_real_type(type);
6849
6850 if (type->checked)
6851 return;
6852
6853 type->checked = TRUE1;
6854
6855 if (type_get_type(type) == TYPE_STRUCT)
6856 {
6857 if (type_is_complete(type))
6858 fields = type_struct_get_fields(type);
6859 else
6860 error_loc_info(&var->loc_info, "undefined type declaration %s\n", type->name);
6861 }
6862 else if (type_get_type(type) == TYPE_UNION || type_get_type(type) == TYPE_ENCAPSULATED_UNION)
6863 fields = type_union_get_cases(type);
6864
6865 if (fields) LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY( field, fields, const var_t, entry )for ((field) = ((const var_t *)((char *)((fields)->next) -
__builtin_offsetof(const var_t, entry))); &(field)->entry
!= (fields); (field) = ((const var_t *)((char *)((field)->
entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof(const var_t, entry))))
6866 if (field->type) check_field_common(type, type->name, field);
6867}
6868
6869/* checks that arguments for a function make sense for marshalling and unmarshalling */
6870static void check_remoting_args(const var_t *func)
6871{
6872 const char *funcname = func->name;
6873 const var_t *arg;
6874
6875 if (func->type->details.function->args) LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY( arg, func->type->details.function->args, const var_t, entry )for ((arg) = ((const var_t *)((char *)((func->type->details
.function->args)->next) - __builtin_offsetof(const var_t
, entry))); &(arg)->entry != (func->type->details
.function->args); (arg) = ((const var_t *)((char *)((arg)->
entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof(const var_t, entry))))
6876 {
6877 const type_t *type = arg->type;
6878
6879 /* check that [out] parameters have enough pointer levels */
6880 if (is_attr(arg->attrs, ATTR_OUT))
6881 {
6882 switch (typegen_detect_type(type, arg->attrs, TDT_ALL_TYPES))
6883 {
6884 case TGT_BASIC:
6885 case TGT_ENUM:
6886 case TGT_RANGE:
6887 case TGT_STRUCT:
6888 case TGT_UNION:
6889 case TGT_CTXT_HANDLE:
6890 case TGT_USER_TYPE:
6891 error_loc_info(&arg->loc_info, "out parameter \'%s\' of function \'%s\' is not a pointer\n", arg->name, funcname);
6892 break;
6893 case TGT_IFACE_POINTER:
6894 error_loc_info(&arg->loc_info, "out interface pointer \'%s\' of function \'%s\' is not a double pointer\n", arg->name, funcname);
6895 break;
6896 case TGT_STRING:
6897 if (is_array(type))
6898 {
6899 /* needs conformance or fixed dimension */
6900 if (type_array_has_conformance(type) &&
6901 type_array_get_conformance(type)->type != EXPR_VOID) break;
6902 if (!type_array_has_conformance(type) && type_array_get_dim(type)) break;
6903 }
6904 if (is_attr( arg->attrs, ATTR_IN )) break;
6905 error_loc_info(&arg->loc_info, "out parameter \'%s\' of function \'%s\' cannot be an unsized string\n", arg->name, funcname);
6906 break;
6907 case TGT_INVALID:
6908 /* already error'd before we get here */
6909 case TGT_CTXT_HANDLE_POINTER:
6910 case TGT_POINTER:
6911 case TGT_ARRAY:
6912 /* OK */
6913 break;
6914 }
6915 }
6916
6917 check_field_common(func->type, funcname, arg);
6918 }
6919
6920 if (type_get_type(type_function_get_rettype(func->type)) != TYPE_VOID)
6921 {
6922 var_t var;
6923 var = *func;
6924 var.type = type_function_get_rettype(func->type);
6925 var.name = xstrdup("return value");
6926 check_field_common(func->type, funcname, &var);
6927 free(var.name);
6928 }
6929}
6930
6931static void add_explicit_handle_if_necessary(const type_t *iface, var_t *func)
6932{
6933 unsigned char explicit_fc, implicit_fc;
6934
6935 /* check for a defined binding handle */
6936 if (!get_func_handle_var( iface, func, &explicit_fc, &implicit_fc ) || !explicit_fc)
6937 {
6938 /* no explicit handle specified so add
6939 * "[in] handle_t IDL_handle" as the first parameter to the
6940 * function */
6941 var_t *idl_handle = make_var(xstrdup("IDL_handle"));
6942 idl_handle->attrs = append_attr(NULL((void*)0), make_attr(ATTR_IN));
6943 idl_handle->type = find_type_or_error("handle_t", 0);
6944 type_function_add_head_arg(func->type, idl_handle);
6945 }
6946}
6947
6948static void check_functions(const type_t *iface, int is_inside_library)
6949{
6950 const statement_t *stmt;
6951 if (is_attr(iface->attrs, ATTR_EXPLICIT_HANDLE))
6952 {
6953 STATEMENTS_FOR_EACH_FUNC( stmt, type_iface_get_stmts(iface) )if (type_iface_get_stmts(iface)) for ((stmt) = ((statement_t *
)((char *)((type_iface_get_stmts(iface))->next) - __builtin_offsetof
(statement_t, entry))); &(stmt)->entry != (type_iface_get_stmts
(iface)); (stmt) = ((statement_t *)((char *)((stmt)->entry
.next) - __builtin_offsetof(statement_t, entry)))) if (stmt->
type == STMT_DECLARATION && stmt->u.var->stgclass
== STG_NONE && type_get_type_detect_alias(stmt->u
.var->type) == TYPE_FUNCTION)
6954 {
6955 var_t *func = stmt->u.var;
6956 add_explicit_handle_if_necessary(iface, func);
6957 }
6958 }
6959 if (!is_inside_library && !is_attr(iface->attrs, ATTR_LOCAL))
6960 {
6961 STATEMENTS_FOR_EACH_FUNC( stmt, type_iface_get_stmts(iface) )if (type_iface_get_stmts(iface)) for ((stmt) = ((statement_t *
)((char *)((type_iface_get_stmts(iface))->next) - __builtin_offsetof
(statement_t, entry))); &(stmt)->entry != (type_iface_get_stmts
(iface)); (stmt) = ((statement_t *)((char *)((stmt)->entry
.next) - __builtin_offsetof(statement_t, entry)))) if (stmt->
type == STMT_DECLARATION && stmt->u.var->stgclass
== STG_NONE && type_get_type_detect_alias(stmt->u
.var->type) == TYPE_FUNCTION)
6962 {
6963 const var_t *func = stmt->u.var;
6964 if (!is_attr(func->attrs, ATTR_LOCAL))
6965 check_remoting_args(func);
6966 }
6967 }
6968}
6969
6970static void check_statements(const statement_list_t *stmts, int is_inside_library)
6971{
6972 const statement_t *stmt;
6973
6974 if (stmts) LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(stmt, stmts, const statement_t, entry)for ((stmt) = ((const statement_t *)((char *)((stmts)->next
) - __builtin_offsetof(const statement_t, entry))); &(stmt
)->entry != (stmts); (stmt) = ((const statement_t *)((char
*)((stmt)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof(const statement_t
, entry))))
6975 {
6976 if (stmt->type == STMT_LIBRARY)
6977 check_statements(stmt->u.lib->stmts, TRUE1);
6978 else if (stmt->type == STMT_TYPE && type_get_type(stmt->u.type) == TYPE_INTERFACE)
6979 check_functions(stmt->u.type, is_inside_library);
6980 }
6981}
6982
6983static void check_all_user_types(const statement_list_t *stmts)
6984{
6985 const statement_t *stmt;
6986
6987 if (stmts) LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY(stmt, stmts, const statement_t, entry)for ((stmt) = ((const statement_t *)((char *)((stmts)->next
) - __builtin_offsetof(const statement_t, entry))); &(stmt
)->entry != (stmts); (stmt) = ((const statement_t *)((char
*)((stmt)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof(const statement_t
, entry))))
6988 {
6989 if (stmt->type == STMT_LIBRARY)
6990 check_all_user_types(stmt->u.lib->stmts);
6991 else if (stmt->type == STMT_TYPE && type_get_type(stmt->u.type) == TYPE_INTERFACE &&
6992 !is_local(stmt->u.type->attrs))
6993 {
6994 const statement_t *stmt_func;
6995 STATEMENTS_FOR_EACH_FUNC(stmt_func, type_iface_get_stmts(stmt->u.type))if (type_iface_get_stmts(stmt->u.type)) for ((stmt_func) =
((statement_t *)((char *)((type_iface_get_stmts(stmt->u.type
))->next) - __builtin_offsetof(statement_t, entry))); &
(stmt_func)->entry != (type_iface_get_stmts(stmt->u.type
)); (stmt_func) = ((statement_t *)((char *)((stmt_func)->entry
.next) - __builtin_offsetof(statement_t, entry)))) if (stmt_func
->type == STMT_DECLARATION && stmt_func->u.var->
stgclass == STG_NONE && type_get_type_detect_alias(stmt_func
->u.var->type) == TYPE_FUNCTION) {
6996 const var_t *func = stmt_func->u.var;
6997 check_for_additional_prototype_types(func->type->details.function->args);
6998 }
6999 }
7000 }
7001}
7002
7003int is_valid_uuid(const char *s)
7004{
7005 int i;
7006
7007 for (i = 0; i < 36; ++i)
7008 if (i == 8 || i == 13 || i == 18 || i == 23)
7009 {
7010 if (s[i] != '-')
7011 return FALSE0;
7012 }
7013 else
7014 if (!isxdigit(s[i])((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) ((s[i]))] & (unsigned short int
) _ISxdigit))
7015 return FALSE0;
7016
7017 return s[i] == '\0';
7018}

7020static statement_t *make_statement(enum statement_type type)
7021{
7022 statement_t *stmt = xmalloc(sizeof(*stmt));
7023 stmt->type = type;
7024 return stmt;
7025}
7026
7027static statement_t *make_statement_type_decl(type_t *type)
7028{
7029 statement_t *stmt = make_statement(STMT_TYPE);
7030 stmt->u.type = type;
7031 return stmt;
7032}
7033
7034static statement_t *make_statement_reference(type_t *type)
7035{
7036 statement_t *stmt = make_statement(STMT_TYPEREF);
7037 stmt->u.type = type;
7038 return stmt;
7039}
7040
7041static statement_t *make_statement_declaration(var_t *var)
7042{
7043 statement_t *stmt = make_statement(STMT_DECLARATION);
7044 stmt->u.var = var;
7045 if (var->stgclass == STG_EXTERN && var->eval)
7046 warning("'%s' initialised and declared extern\n", var->name);
7047 if (is_const_decl(var))
7048 {
7049 if (var->eval)
7050 reg_const(var);
7051 }
7052 else if (type_get_type(var->type) == TYPE_FUNCTION)
7053 check_function_attrs(var->name, var->attrs);
7054 else if (var->stgclass == STG_NONE || var->stgclass == STG_REGISTER)
7055 error_loc("instantiation of data is illegal\n");
7056 return stmt;
7057}

7059static statement_t *make_statement_library(typelib_t *typelib)
7060{
7061 statement_t *stmt = make_statement(STMT_LIBRARY);
7062 stmt->u.lib = typelib;
7063 return stmt;
7064}

7100
7101static statement_t *make_statement_typedef(declarator_list_t *decls)
7102{
7103 declarator_t *decl, *next;
7104 statement_t *stmt;
7105 type_list_t **type_list;
7106
7107 if (!decls) return NULL((void*)0);
7108
7109 stmt = make_statement(STMT_TYPEDEF);
7110 stmt->u.type_list = NULL((void*)0);
7111 type_list = &stmt->u.type_list;
7112
7113 LIST_FOR_EACH_ENTRY_SAFE( decl, next, decls, declarator_t, entry )for ((decl) = ((declarator_t *)((char *)((decls)->next) - __builtin_offsetof
(declarator_t, entry))), (next) = ((declarator_t *)((char *)(
(decl)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof(declarator_t, entry
))); &(decl)->entry != (decls); (decl) = (next), (next
) = ((declarator_t *)((char *)((decl)->entry.next) - __builtin_offsetof
(declarator_t, entry))))
7114 {
7115 var_t *var = decl->var;
7116 type_t *type = find_type_or_error(var->name, 0);
7117 *type_list = xmalloc(sizeof(type_list_t));
7118 (*type_list)->type = type;
7119 (*type_list)->next = NULL((void*)0);
7120
7121 type_list = &(*type_list)->next;
7122 free(decl);
7123 free(var);
7124 }
7125
7126 return stmt;
7127}
7128
7129static statement_list_t *append_statements(statement_list_t *l1, statement_list_t *l2)
7130{
7131 if (!l2) return l1;
7132 if (!l1 || l1 == l2) return l2;
7133 list_move_tail (l1, l2);
7134 return l1;
7135}
7136
7137static attr_list_t *append_attribs(attr_list_t *l1, attr_list_t *l2)
7138{
7139 if (!l2) return l1;
7140 if (!l1 || l1 == l2) return l2;
7141 list_move_tail (l1, l2);
7142 return l1;
7143}
7144
7145static statement_list_t *append_statement(statement_list_t *list, statement_t *stmt)
7146{
7147 if (!stmt) return list;
7148 if (!list)
7149 {
7150 list = xmalloc( sizeof(*list) );
7151 list_init( list );
7152 }
7153 list_add_tail( list, &stmt->entry );
7154 return list;
7155}

7157void init_loc_info(loc_info_t *i)
7158{
7159 i->input_name = input_name ? input_name : "stdin";
7160 i->line_number = line_number;
7161 i->near_text = parser_text;
7162}
7163
7164static void check_def(const type_t *t)
7165{
7166 if (t->defined)
7167 error_loc("%s: redefinition error; original definition was at %s:%d\n",
7168 t->name, t->loc_info.input_name, t->loc_info.line_number);
7169}
